# SpongeJIT No-Interpreter Design Reset

## Key Code

### PVM grounding

PVM guide says handler-form phases must return triplets and install methods only for handled ASDL types:

```lua
-- PVM_GUIDE.md lines 415-420
Handlers receive a node and **must return a triplet** ...
If a handler has no output, return `pvm.empty()`.
Returning `nil` from a handler is an error.
```

```lua
-- PVM_GUIDE.md lines 518-528
After `pvm.phase(name, handlers)`, every handled ASDL type gains a method
`:name(...)` returning the triplet directly:
...
Extra arguments are allowed and become part of the cache key:
```

Scalar phases are separate:

```lua
-- PVM_GUIDE.md lines 557-563, 589-591
Use `pvm.phase(name, handlers)` when boundary output is a stream...
Use `pvm.phase(name, fn)` + `pvm.one(...)` when boundary output is a single value...
A scalar boundary is just phase in function form.
```

Flattening expectation:

```text
-- PVM_GUIDE.md lines 1628-1631
□ Cmd type is uniform (one product, Kind singleton)
□ Containment is push/pop markers
□ For-loop execution (no recursive dispatch)
□ State is push/pop stacks only
```

### Current ASDL layers

Schema doctrine explicitly separates layers:

```asdl
-- spongejit_lua_ssa.asdl lines 9-15
--   LuaSrc       answers: what did PUC encode?
--   LuaEvidence answers: what did runtime/foundry prove and lease?
--   LuaSem      answers: what does that bytecode mean under that evidence?
--   LuaNF       answers: what is the least equivalent semantic computation?
--   LuaContract answers: what facts/exits/projections are required/transferred?
--   LuaPlace    answers: where may already-reduced values live?
--   MoonOut     answers: what Moonlift-level kernel boundary is emitted.
```

Important current protocol/output types:

```asdl
-- spongejit_lua_ssa.asdl lines 483-543
Exit = GuardExit(...)
     | ReturnExit(...)
     | Return0Exit(...)
     | JumpExit(...)
     | ConditionalJumpExit(...)
     | TestSetExit(...)
     | LoopRegionExit(...)
     | CallProtocolExit(...)
     | CloseProtocolExit(...)
     | GenericForProtocolExit(...)
     | SetListProtocolExit(...)
     | GetVargProtocolExit(...)
```

```asdl
-- spongejit_lua_ssa.asdl lines 620-640
module MoonOut {
    AbiValue = ExecCtx | StackPtr | ConstPtr | UpvaluePtr | PrimitiveTable
    KernelKind = InlineSpan | FunctionFastPath
    Param = (string name, string moon_type) unique
    Projection = (LuaNF.Exit exit, LuaNF.Projection* obligations) unique
    Kernel = (MoonOut.KernelKind kind,
              MoonOut.Param* params,
              LuaNF.Program normal_form,
              LuaContract.Contract contract,
              MoonOut.Projection* projections) unique
}
```

Observation: `MoonOut.Kernel` still carries full `LuaNF.Program`, not a stripped flat command array.

### Current scalar PVM boundaries

All LuaCompile boundaries found are scalar `pvm.phase(name, fn)` + `pvm.one`, not handler-form phases:

```lua
-- lua_compile_to_normal_form.lua lines 13-26
local function compile_value(unit)
  local sem = SemLower.lower(unit.source, unit.evidence)
  if pvm.classof(sem) == T.LuaSem.Rejected then return T.LuaCompile.Reject(sem.rejection) end
  local nf = NFNormalize.normalize(sem.program)
  local contract = ContractDerive.derive(nf)
  return T.LuaCompile.Ok(T.LuaCompile.NormalForm(nf, contract))
end

local phase = pvm.phase("spongejit_lua_compile_to_normal_form", function(unit)
  return compile_value(unit)
end)

function M.compile(unit)
  return pvm.one(phase(unit))
end
```

Other scalar phases:
- `lua_src_to_lua_sem_lower.lua` lines 681-686
- `lua_sem_to_lua_nf_normalize.lua` lines 242-247
- `lua_nf_to_lua_contract_derive.lua` lines 105-110
- `lua_nf_to_moon_out_lower.lua` lines 18-23
- `lua_compile_to_moon_kernel.lua` lines 19-24

No `pvm.once`, `pvm.empty`, `pvm.children`, `pvm.drain`, or `pvm.each` usage appears in `spongejit/lua_compile`; tests assert scalar phase cache stats instead.

### Current protocol exits

LuaSem emits protocol observations for dynamic Lua operations:

```lua
-- lua_src_to_lua_sem_lower.lua lines 482-527
add_decision("CALL", "semantic", function(ctx, op)
  ctx.effects[#ctx.effects + 1] = Sem.Observe(Sem.CallProtocolObservation(...))
end)
...
add_decision("SETLIST", "semantic", function(ctx, op)
  ctx.effects[#ctx.effects + 1] = Sem.Observe(Sem.SetListProtocolObservation(...))
end)
...
add_decision("GETVARG", "semantic", function(ctx, op)
  ctx.effects[#ctx.effects + 1] = Sem.Observe(Sem.GetVargProtocolObservation(...))
end)
```

Normalizer turns these into NF exits:

```lua
-- lua_sem_to_lua_nf_normalize.lua lines 194-212
elseif obs.kind == "CallProtocolObservation" then
  local exit = NF.CallProtocolExit(...)
...
elseif obs.kind == "CloseProtocolObservation" then
  local exit = NF.CloseProtocolExit(...)
...
elseif obs.kind == "GenericForProtocolObservation" then
  local exit = NF.GenericForProtocolExit(...)
...
elseif obs.kind == "SetListProtocolObservation" then
  local exit = NF.SetListProtocolExit(...)
...
elseif obs.kind == "GetVargProtocolObservation" then
  local exit = NF.GetVargProtocolExit(...)
```

MoonOut emission maps them to output tags:

```lua
-- moon_out_emit.lua lines 307-349
elseif cls == NF.CallProtocolExit then
  lines[#lines + 1] = "    out_tag[0] = " .. Abi.TAG.call
...
elseif cls == NF.CloseProtocolExit then
  lines[#lines + 1] = "    out_tag[0] = " .. Abi.TAG.close
...
elseif cls == NF.GenericForProtocolExit then
  lines[#lines + 1] = "    out_tag[0] = " .. Abi.TAG.generic_for
...
elseif cls == NF.SetListProtocolExit then
  lines[#lines + 1] = "    out_tag[0] = " .. Abi.TAG.setlist
...
elseif cls == NF.GetVargProtocolExit then
  lines[#lines + 1] = "    out_tag[0] = " .. Abi.TAG.getvarg
```

### Current rejection model

Structured rejection is an ASDL result:

```asdl
-- spongejit_lua_ssa.asdl lines 368-388
RejectionReason = ContradictoryEvidence
                | MissingFact
                | MissingPayloadLease
                | UnsupportedOpcode
                | UnsupportedFactCombination
                | UnsupportedSemanticCase
                | UnsupportedLoopRegion
                | UnsupportedProjection
                | InternalInvariantFailure

Result = Accepted(LuaSem.Program program) unique
       | Rejected(LuaSem.Rejection rejection) unique
```

Lowering rejects on contradiction, unsupported opcode, missing evidence, unsupported semantic cases:

```lua
-- lua_src_to_lua_sem_lower.lua lines 653-678
local contradictions = Contradiction.find(evidence)
if #contradictions > 0 then ... return reject(..., "contradictory_evidence") end
...
if op.kind == "UnsupportedOpcode" then return reject(op, "unsupported_opcode") end
local decision = DECISION[op.kind]
if not decision then return reject(op, "unsupported_opcode") end
local result = decision(ctx, op)
if result then return result end
...
return Sem.Accepted(Sem.Program(...))
```

Runtime fact-required fast paths reject with `MissingFact`/`MissingPayloadLease` rather than fallback helpers.

```lua
M.TAG = {

  branch = 5,
  call = 6,
  close = 7,
  generic_for = 8,
  setlist = 9,
  getvarg = 10,
}
```

```lua
-- moon_out_abi.lua lines 74-98
M.PROTOCOL_PARAMS = {
  { "out_tag", "ptr(i32)" },
  { "out_value_kind", "ptr(i32)" },
  { "out_pc", "ptr(i64)" },
  ...
  { "out_event_count", "ptr(i32)" },
}
```

Emission produces one Moonlift function with pointer out-params:

```lua
-- moon_out_emit.lua lines 416-446
local name = opts.name or "lua_compile_kernel"
lines[#lines + 1] = "local " .. name .. " = func(" .. param_sig(kernel.params) .. ") -> i32"
...
for _, step in ipairs(kernel.normal_form.steps or {}) do
  ...
  elseif cls == NF.StepExit then emit_exit(lines, step.exit); saw_terminal = true; break end
end
...
return table.concat(lines, "\n")
```

## Relationships

Data flow currently is:

```text
PUC event tables
  -> lua_src_from_puc_decode.decode
  -> LuaSrc.Window
  -> LuaCompile.Unit(source, evidence)
  -> lua_src_to_lua_sem_lower.lower(window, evidence)
       returns LuaSem.Accepted(program) or LuaSem.Rejected(rejection)
  -> lua_sem_to_lua_nf_normalize.normalize(program)
       turns observations into LuaNF.Step/LuaNF.Exit
  -> lua_nf_to_lua_contract_derive.derive(nf)
       derives facts, payload uses, projection obligations, deps
  -> lua_compile_to_normal_form.compile(unit)
       returns LuaCompile.Ok(NormalForm(nf, contract)) or Reject
  -> lua_nf_to_moon_out_lower.lower(nf, contract)
       wraps NF+contract into MoonOut.Kernel
  -> moon_out_emit.emit(kernel)
       emits Moonlift source function using out_* pointer protocol
```

Foundry path:

```text
windows + fact bundles
  -> lua_compile_foundry.compile_window
  -> compile_to_normal_form
  -> NFKey + ContractKey representative_key
  -> compile_to_moon_kernel
  -> MoonOut emission
  -> artifacts: representatives, alias_map, grammar_coverage
```

PVM boundary style:

```text
All current LuaCompile phases = scalar phase form.
They cache by ASDL identity plus extra args:
  SemLower.lower(window, evidence)
  MoonLower.lower(nf, contract)
No handler-form pvm.phase table was found in lua_compile, so no ASDL :method installation is currently used.
```

## Observations

- Current schema has many ASDL layers, all `unique`, but `MoonOut.Kernel` retains `LuaNF.Program` and `LuaContract.Contract`; it is not a PVM-guide-style final uniform flat `Cmd` product array.
- Current MoonOut output is a tag/pointer protocol (`out_tag`, `out_value_kind`, etc.) rather than a flat command list consumed by a simple for-loop.
- Protocol handoffs are currently modeled as successful compiled outputs: CALL, TAILCALL, CLOSE/TBC, TFOR*, SETLIST, GETVARG all become NF protocol exits and MoonOut tags.
- Tests encode that protocol-exit behavior as expected success, especially `test_spongejit_lua_compile_moon_out.lua` lines 376-417.
- Tests also encode “no hidden helpers/fake boundary” for guard exits and truthiness (`test_spongejit_lua_compile_moon_out.lua` lines 428-457).
- `test_spongejit_lua_compile_completion.lua` is currently red. Running it produced:
  - `generic ADD -> MissingFact`
  - `generic GETTABLE -> MissingFact`
  - `generic SETTABLE -> MissingFact`
  - `generic LEN -> MissingFact`
  - `generic CONCAT -> MissingFact`
  - `variable-count VARARG -> UnsupportedSemanticCase`
  - `multivalue RETURN -> UnsupportedSemanticCase`
  - `ERRNNIL runtime check -> MissingFact`
- A direct decision-count check showed current `Lower.decision_for` reports `semantic` for all 85 real `LuaSrc.Op` variants and `reject` for 0; rejections now occur inside semantic handlers due to evidence/semantic limits.
- Makefile quarantines old SSA/stencil/bank path and has `no-old-imports` checks against `src.ssa`, `stencil_`, `SponDesc`, `sponbank`, `OpcodeHelper`, `HelperCall`, etc. 
- `test_spongejit_lua_compile_foundry.lua` asserts old `src.ssa`, `src.ssa_ir`, `src.ssa_to_stencil`, `src.stencil_lower` are not loaded and that ADDI/ADDK dedupe by `LuaNF+LuaContract`, not source opcode chain.
- `test_spongejit_lua_compile_pipeline.lua` asserts PVM scalar phase cache hits for each phase; this is the strongest current method/phase-boundary test.
- `test_spongejit_lua_compile_moon_out.lua` asserts `MoonOut must not receive PUC opcode-shaped code` by recursively checking for `LuaSrc.Op` inside the kernel; however, `MoonOut.Kernel` still contains NF that was derived from source.
